It does not attempt to cover everything in bootstrap, but rather offer the most common elements as shortcuts. Sometimes, when you want something more specific or fancy, you can still use the original bootstrap markup.\n    </i>\n   </p>\n   <h3>\n    Usage\n   </h3>\n   <p>\n    Downloads:\n   </p>\n   <ul>\n
